YIELD: 12 Servings
EACH PORTION: 1 Slice
PAN SIZE: 10x15" Jelly Roll Pan
TEMPERATURE: 350Â° F. Oven

METHOD:

Chocolate Cake:
Grease and flour a 10x15" jelly roll pan. In a large bowl, sift together flour, sugar, baking soda, cinnamon, and salt. In a saucepan, combine margarine, shortening, cocoa, and water. Bring to boil. Cook for 1 minute. Pour over the dry ingredients. Stir well. Blend in beaten eggs and buttermilk. Pour into the jelly roll pan. Bake at 350 degrees F for 30 minutes, or until toothpick inserted into center of cake comes out clean. Let cool.

Cream Cheese Icing:
In a saucepan, on meadium-low heat, melt butter and cream cheese. Take off heat and combine with the vanilla extract and powdered sugar. Mix until smooth and spread on cake.

Cut into 12 slices before serving.

YIELD: 12 Servings
EACH PORTION: 1 Slice
PAN SIZE: 10x15" Jelly Roll Pan
TEMPERATURE: 350Â° F. Oven

METHOD:

Chocolate Cake:
Grease and flour a 10x15" jelly roll pan. In a large bowl, sift together flour, sugar, baking soda, cinnamon, and salt. In a saucepan, combine margarine, shortening, cocoa, and water. Bring to boil. Cook for 1 minute. Pour over the dry ingredients. Stir well. Blend in beaten eggs and buttermilk. Pour into the jelly roll pan. Bake in a 350 degree F. oven for 30 minutes, or until toothpick inserted into center of cake comes out clean. Let cool.

Vanilla Icing:
In large bowl combine powdered sugar, shortening, milk, flour, salt and vanilla extract. Beat at low speed with an electric mixer for 45 seconds or until blended. Increase to high speed and beat for 3 - 5 minutes or until smooth and creamy. Spread on cake.

Marble Cake:

YIELD: 8 Servings
PAN SIZE: 9x13" Baking Dish
TEMPERATURE: 350Â° F. Oven

METHOD:

Crepes:
In a medium bowl, thoroughly beat eggs. Add milk and melted butter. Beat in flour and salt. Mix until smooth. Let batter set .5 hour. Pour batter into medium hot skillet, making 8 crepes, 6-8 inches in circumference. Brown and set aside.

Meat Filling:
In a large skillet, over medium heat, brown veall, ground chicken (substituted roasted, chopped chicken in recipe), and 1/2 lb raw beef in butter. Stir in minced parsley, cheese, salt, ground pepper, and nutmeg. Let cool.

White Sauce:
In a small saucepan, over medium heat, cook flour and butter together for 1 minute. Stir in salt, ground pepper, and nutmeg. Then, stir in milk and continue to cook until thick.

Presentation:
Spread one-half of the 32 oz. jar tomato pasta sauce (substituted Ready-To-Serve Spaghetti/Marinara Sauce in recipe) in bottom of baking dish. Fill crepes with meat mixture, folding over all sides of crepe to form palm-sized bundles. Place seam side down in baking dish. Cover with remaining tomato pasta sauce and pour White Sauce over everthing. Cover with mozzarella cheese first, then with parmesan cheese. Bake in a 9x13" baking pan, in a 375 degree F oven for 20 to 30 minutes, or until cheese is bubbly and brown on the edges. Serve.]]></memo></recipe><recipe createDate="05/13/2003" description="Dish, manicotti w/cheese filling" modifyDate="05/13/2003" nutrientRefNum="539815152" primaryKey="539815152" recordType="insert" YIELD: 6 Servings

METHOD:

Spaghetti Noodles:
Fill large cooking pot with 7qts water. Bring to boil. Add pasta to boiling water. Cook 8 - 10 minutes or until al dente. Drain. Do not rinse.

Spaghetti Sauce:
Heat olive oil in Dutch oven. Cook and stir onion and finely chopped garlic until onion is tender. Stir in 3-8oz cans tomato sauce, 1-4oz can mushrooms with liquid, green pepper, parsley, salt, ground pepper, sugar, dry basil leaves, and oregano. Heat to boiling, reduce heat. Cover and simmer, stirring occasionally, for 1 hour. Stir in dry red wine. Cover and simmer, stirring occasionally, for 30 minutes. 

Meatballs:
Mix together 1.5 lb raw ground beef, bread crumbs, finely chopped onion, milk, dry red wine, egg, parsley, salt, Worcestershire Sauce, and ground pepper. Shape into rounded tablespoon size balls. Heat 1/4 cup canola oil (2 tablespoons used in nutritional anaylsis) in 10-inch skillet. Cook meatballs in hot oil until done, about 20 minutes.

YIELD: 6 Servings
EACH PORTION: 2 Cups

METHOD:

Slice 1 large onion. Chop 2 stalks celery including leaves, and 3 large carrots into 1-inch chunks. Place carrots, onion, celery, and 6 lbs beef soup bones in large, shallow roasting pan. Bake, uncovered & turning occasionally, for 30 minutes or until bones are well browned.

After bones are browned, drain off excess fat. Place contents of roasting pan into large soup pot or Dutch oven. Pour .5 cup water into roasting pan and rinse. Pour this liquid into soup pot. Add l large tomato, 1/2 cup chopped parsnip, 1/2 cup cubed potatoes, 8 whole black peppercorns, 4 sprigs fresh parsley, 1 bay leaf, 1 tbsp salt, 2 tsp dried thyme, 2 cloves garlic and 12 cups water. Bring mixture to a boil. Reduce heat. Cover and simmer for 5 hours. Strain stock. Discard meat, vegetables, and seasonings.

TO CLARIFY STOCK:
To remove pieces too small to be strained out with cheesecloth, combine .25 cup cold water, 1 egg white, and 1 crushed eggshell. Add to strained stock. Bring to a boil. Remove from heat. Let stand 5 minutes. Strain again through sieve lined with cheesecloth.]]></memo></recipe><recipe createDate="05/13/2003" description="Soup, menudo, Mexican beef soup" modifyDate="05/13/2003" nutrientRefNum="220365900" primaryKey="220365900" recordType="insert" useStaticIngrStmt="false" userCode="32216" version="2.2.0"><labelOption buildInsigFootnote="true" calcDVRaw="true" hide449Footnote="false" hideGramWeight="false" hideInsigFootnote="false" hideServings="false" labelDVStandard="1" labelElementType="0" labelFootnoteOrientation="1.000000" labelStyleFormat="0" rrUSCalories="0" rrUSCaloriesFat="0" rrUSCarbs="0" rrUSCholesterol="0" rrUSProtein="0" rrUSSugars="0" rrUSVitMin="0" showStandardFootnote="true" useAbbrev="false"><languageOption languageEnum="1" servingSizeText="" servingsContainerText=""/></labelOption><labelPageLayout labelPageObjectHeight="0" labelPageObjectLeft="0.500000" labelPageObjectTop="0.500000" labelPageObjectType="2" labelPageObjectWidth="1.930000"/><labelPageLayout labelPageObjectHeight="0" labelPageObjectLeft="4.000000" labelPageObjectTop="2.000000" labelPageObjectType="3" labelPageObjectWidth="0.860000"/><labelPageLayout labelPageObjectHeight="0" labelPageObjectLeft="4.000000" labelPageObjectTop="2.000000" labelPageObjectType="4" labelPageObjectWidth="0.660000"/><GroupData><Group groupName="COMMON"/></GroupData><Yield cookedYield="100" percentRefuse="0" yieldKey="1"><measure gramWeight="-1.000000" measureKey="31" quantity="12.000000"/></Yield><RecipeItem ItemName="Beef Tripe-Cooked" itemDataType="1" itemDisplayOrder="0" itemEshaCode="10089" itemKey="10089" itemMeasureKey="7" itemQuantity="6.000000" itemQuantityText="" itemYieldKey="1"/><RecipeItem ItemName="Water" itemDataType="1" itemDisplayOrder="1" itemEshaCode="20041" itemKey="20041" itemMeasureKey="3" itemQuantity="16.000000" itemQuantityText="" itemYieldKey="1"/><RecipeItem ItemName="White Onions-Raw-Med-Whole-2 1/2&quot; YIELDS: 24
EACH PORTION: 1 Roll
PAN SIZE: 9x13" Baking Dish
TEMPERATURE: 375Â° F. Oven

METHOD:

1. In saucepan, heat 1 cup milk, water and 1/4 cup butter until very warm (butter doesn't need to be completely melted). Remove from heat.

2. Mix together salt, flour, yeast, 1/2 cup sugar, eggs and 1/3 cup softened butter in a medium bowl. Add the heated mixture until mixed well.

3. Divide dough into two parts. On a floured surface, roll each part into a large rectangle. Smear each rectangle with softened butter. Combine the cinnamon and 3/4 cup sugar. Sprinkle over the rectangles. Generously sprinkle the raisins and nuts over the top.

4. Roll the dough up into two logs starting at the long side. Cut each log into 12 slices. Place the rolls cut side down into to a  9 x 13-inch greased baking pans. Cover, and let rise in a warm place until almost doubled (about 30 minutes).

5. Bake in a preheated 375Â° F oven for 20 to 25 minutes, or until golden brown.

6. To make the frosting: Combine the powdered sugar, 3 tablespoons melted butter, vanilla and 3 tablespoons milk. Frosting should be thick. Spread over baked rolls.

(Note: Recipe calls to use bread machine to mix dough, mixing by hand substituted above.)]]></memo></recipe><recipe createDate="05/13/2003" description="Taco, chicken" modifyDate="02/05/2009"
